***doem.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doem.html>doem</a> (49682)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*duom</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dōmaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰóh₁mos</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:doem.html>doem</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">doom</i>, Danish and Swedish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:dom.html>dom</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>doom, condemnation</li></ol>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">doemdenken</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">doemdenker</span></li>

***doemen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doemen.html>doemen</a> (94066)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doemen.html>doemen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">duomen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dōmijaną</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to doom, to condemn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gedoemd.html>gedoemd</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdwijnen.html>verdwijnen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> are <b>doomed</b> to perish.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***doen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a> (63)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">duon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dōną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰéh₁t</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to do</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>Doe</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> in.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Just <b>put</b> it in there.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause to, to make; <span class="use-with-mention">forms causative verbs</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:denken.html>denken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorig.html>vorig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <b><a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> think of last year; i.e. that reminds <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> of last year.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elkaar.html>elkaar</a></i> + indefinite pronoun, sometimes with postpositioned <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be different; to make a difference
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beide.html>beide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:camera.html>camera</a>'s <b><a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:elkaar.html>elkaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a>).</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The two <a href = vnd.unilang:cameras.html>cameras</a> <b>are</b>n’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> much <b>different</b> [i.e. neither <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> much better than the other].</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with an adjective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to behave or act in some way
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>Doe</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewoon.html>gewoon</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Just <b>act</b> normal.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Used as the finite verb after the fronting of an infinitive.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>Werken</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> work anymore.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>routine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schikken.html>schikken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The people are outside of their <b>routine</b>, but do accommodate themselves.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***dof.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dof.html>dof</a> (31973)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doof.html>doof</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dōf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*daubaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stunned, deaf</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰewbʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to whisk, be obscured</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:dov.html>dov</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:matt.html>matt</a>, muted</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dowf</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dof.html>dof</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doffer.html>doffer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">dofst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">surface</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dull, <a href = vnd.unilang:matte.html>matte</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sound</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dull, muffled</li>
<li>languid, apathetic
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">loom</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lui.html>lui</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flauw.html>flauw</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">mat</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***dokter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dokter.html>dokter</a> (409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">doctor</i>, assimilated to Dutch phonetics through common use, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">doctoor</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">doctor</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dokter.html>dokter</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dokters.html>dokters</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doktoren.html>doktoren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doktertje.html>doktertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>doctor <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">physician, medical doctor</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***doktor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doktor.html>doktor</a> (15972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">doctor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">doctor (person who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> attained a doctorate)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">doctor</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">doctor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">teacher, instructor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="id"><a href = vnd.unilang:dokter.html>dokter</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_11">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="id"><a href = vnd.unilang:doktor.html>doktor</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>doctor (person who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> attained a doctorate)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> part of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Comparison_of_Standard_Malay_and_Indonesian" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Comparison of Standard Malay and Indonesian">false friends between Standard Malay and Indonesian</a> due to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/False_friend" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:False friend">shared etymology</a>. The Brunei, Malaysia and Singapore usage can be seen in Malay <span class="Latn" lang="ms"><a href = vnd.unilang:doktor.html>doktor</a></span>.
</p>

***dol.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dol.html>dol</a> (1271)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:dol.html>dol</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dulaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dol.html>dol</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doller.html>doller</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">dolst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crazy, silly, mad</li>
<li>mindless, reckless; irate</li>
<li>out of control, <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a> wild, notably <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> of a tool or machine</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">doldraaien</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">verb</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">doldwaas</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">adj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dolheid.html>dolheid</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">dollekoeienziekte</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þullaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dol.html>dol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dollen.html>dollen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dolletje.html>dolletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A thole(-pin); sometimes also used for a similarly functioning cutout in the gunwhale.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">delfijn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">delphīnus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">δελφίς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">delphís</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dolphin</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dolheid.html>dolheid</a> (107536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dulheit</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dol.html>dol</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crazy; mad, insane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dolheid.html>dolheid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dolheid.html>dolheden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dolheid.html>dolheidje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Madness, insanity</li>
<li>Mental craziness, folly</li>
<li>Any strong, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> excessive emotional state:
<ol><li>extasis</li>
<li>passion</li>
<li>fury, rage</li></ol></li>
<li>(<a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>Nick</a>)name of various diseases which cause excessive behavior such as rage</li></ol>

***dollen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dollen.html>dollen</a> (7219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dollen.html>dollen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dullen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dol.html>dol</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, next to older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dolen.html>dolen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dollen.html>dollen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tomfool, to fool around, to frolick, to play
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vader.html>vader</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dolde.html>dolde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the dad <b>played</b> with his children</span></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mess with, take the mikey out of someone</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stun (cattle) with a blow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rage, act outrageously</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:dolle.html>dolle</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dig a hole</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***dom.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dom.html>dom</a> (972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dom.html>dom</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">dumb</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dumbaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dom.html>dom</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dommer.html>dommer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">domst</b>)

<ol><li>dumb, brainless</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doem.html>doem</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:domus.html>domus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house, building</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dṓm</i>, from root <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dem-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to build</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cf. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">duom</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dom.html>dom</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dommen.html>dommen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dom.html>dommetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>) (only domkerken, domkerkje)<span id="attentionseekingnl" class="attentionseeking" lang="nl" title="what | s going on here?"></span>
</p>
<ol><li>domkerk<span id="attentionseekingnl" class="attentionseeking" lang="nl" title="not an English word, shouldn | t be used in a gloss"></span>, either an episcopal cathedral or another major church (often a basilica) which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> granted this high rank</li></ol>

***dommekracht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dommekracht.html>dommekracht</a> (83937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dom.html>dom</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thumb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kracht.html>kracht</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dommekracht.html>dommekracht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dommekrachten.html>dommekrachten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dommekracht.html>dommekrachtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> suited for lifting heavy loads</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dumb strong person, similar to <a href = vnd.unilang:gorilla.html>gorilla</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">duimkracht</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">keldervijs</span></li>

***donder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:donder.html>donder</a> (1689)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">donre</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:donner.html>donner</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:donder.html>donder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thunar</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thonar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þunraz</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)tenh₂-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:donner.html>Donner</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tonger</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thunder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:donder.html>donder</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>thunder <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">sound produced by a thunderstorm</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a thing (as in <i>not a single thing</i>)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haalt.html>haalt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:donder.html>donder</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a>!</i>
<dl><dd>What you're doing right now isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> achieving <b>a thing</b>!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">donresdach</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">donredach</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thonaresdag</i>, from late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*Þunras dagaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">day of <a href = vnd.unilang:thor.html>Thor</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Dunnersdag</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Donnerstag</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tongersdei</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Thursday</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">torsdag</i>.
</p>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:donderdag.html>donderdag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thursday</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">morning</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***donderen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:donderen.html>donderen</a> (32705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">donren</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:donderen.html>donderen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:donder.html>donder</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:donderen.html>donderen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to thunder
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verte.html>verte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:donderen.html>donderen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I can hear it <b>thunder</b> in the distance.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a thunderous sound, especially with one's voice
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">'<a href = vnd.unilang:hou.html>Hou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a>!', <b><a href = vnd.unilang:donderde.html>donderde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">'<a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>Stop</a> that right now!', <b>thundered</b> the <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to plummet, tumble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leerling.html>leerling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verloor.html>verloor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:evenwicht.html>evenwicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:donderde.html>donderde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterover.html>achterover</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The pupil <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> his balance and <b>tumbled</b> backwards off his chair.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">afdonderen</span></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:donker.html>donker</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dunker.html>dunker</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dunkal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dunkalaz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dunkaraz</i>.
</p>
